\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ \textcolor{comment}{/**********************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ raymath\ v1.5\ -\/\ Math\ functions\ to\ work\ with\ Vector2,\ Vector3,\ Matrix\ and\ Quaternions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ CONFIGURATION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RAYMATH\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Generates\ the\ implementation\ of\ the\ library\ into\ the\ included\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ not\ defined,\ the\ library\ is\ in\ header\ only\ mode\ and\ can\ be\ included\ in\ other\ headers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ or\ source\ files\ without\ problems.\ But\ only\ ONE\ file\ should\ hold\ the\ implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RAYMATH\_STATIC\_INLINE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Define\ static\ inline\ functions\ code,\ so\ \#include\ header\ suffices\ for\ use.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ This\ may\ use\ up\ lots\ of\ memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ CONVENTIONS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Functions\ are\ always\ self-\/contained,\ no\ function\ use\ another\ raymath\ function\ inside,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ required\ code\ is\ directly\ re-\/implemented\ inside}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Functions\ input\ parameters\ are\ always\ received\ by\ value\ (2\ unavoidable\ exceptions)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Functions\ use\ always\ a\ "{}result"{}\ variable\ for\ return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Functions\ are\ always\ defined\ inline}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Angles\ are\ always\ in\ radians\ (DEG2RAD/RAD2DEG\ macros\ provided\ for\ convenience)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
